<Name>Martin Veneroso (slickmv)<//Name>< text>
New owners, new hours (9:00am - 9:30pm, seven days), newly freshened interior. The menu has been revamped also, but the contents seem very similar if not exactly the same; I'll try to get photos of the menu next time.

They still have bargain prices for pho; you won't get as much meat as at other places that cost more, so you have to decide if the trade off is worth it to you.

Supposedly the kitchen staff is unchanged. Certainly the pho broth seems very similar to me, a little sweeter than I would prefer, but still quite good.< /text>

<Name>Chevy Nation<//Name><gmap_id>0x80dd289534c4c841:0xbe1db5847d6d55a7< /gmap_id><response>None<//response><pics>None<//pics>< text>
This place is the best place by far that I have ever been to. I drive all the way from Laguna Beach to come here for their amazing food. Their prices are excellent and I enjoy the way I am treated and served. They treat you like family here and are so nice in person and over the phone. The place is clean and again the food is by far the best pho I have ever had and their spring rolls are great too. They don't come apart like other places and they accommodate vegetarians with substitute items available. I wouldn't drive this far if I didn't think the prices were worth it or the quality of food. I am so glad I found this place years and years ago! Thanks pho lam son!<//text>

<rate>5< /rate><Text>Jerrad at Noble Gold Investments is without a doubt fantastic, thoughtful as well as informative with a contagiously unambiguous demeanor.
Here's why:
I have always been a fact finder. If I don't feel information is correct, I look elsewhere. Since covid, it is clear the news media is not making sense, is biased and causing me to pay close attention to market sentiments as well.
I changed my news source to a truth source some time ago and currently listen to the X22 Report with Dave. I really enjoy his commentary, because I can confirm what he says and he is pleasant to listen too.
It just happens that Noble Gold Investments is one of the advertisements that X22 Report presents. While I used TD Ameritrade (solid company), I could not buy precious metals there, and my gut was saying the stock market could fall..., again.
Now, I'm not the smartest at stocks, but I did know I could secure my current investments with gold, but my knowledge in precious metals investments is not so great.
The other day X22 Reprt showed Noble Gold Investments during one of its ads. I jotted down Noble Gold‚Äôs number and made a call to get answers to my seemingly endless questions.

< review>
Swig is a fun club-type atmosphere that seems to cater to the bridge and tunnel folk mostly. if you're in the mood to be starred at and questioned as to why you're there then this is the spot for you. Put on your fancy dress and high-heels and get yourself downtown to Swig.

The contemporary decor seems to keep up to date and thrives as being a sophisticated bar. I think it's lacking in the classy aspect of the word sophistication. Although, the drinks are good and music is fine, there seems to be nothing special or deserving of a 4th star.

When there's a good DJ or live music then it's a better night. Be sure to check it out for your own experience.< /review>

< Text>
Use them if YOU WANT to MISS YOUR FLIGHT.

We received couple of reservation confirmation emails on May.14 from Executive Car Service (E.C.S.) for a R/T transportation between Malibu-LAX, starting on Jun.10. 12PM.

On Jun.8, I called the E.C.S. to confirm the reservation; we received a following confirmation email that the company designated a driver for the Jun.10 12pm pickup.

Our experience with other Car Service companies have been that the company made a phone call few hours before our trip followed by a confirmation call by their driver on their way to our house with an estimated approaching time, NOT this company.

Not hearing from them, at 11:50AM, I called the company, was informed that the designated driver's car was broken (without informing us); a substitute driver was on its way, about 40minutes away!
We rejected their service; tried to find a local Taxi, none available at the time, so we jumped in our car and rushed to the LAX; eventually found a parking lot with a free spot (these days, parking lots require a reservation).

Driving to LAX was very stressful because of the time strain; we would had missed our River Cruise boat if missed the flight, consequently a costly trip to reach the boat.  Thanks to the flight delay, we made it, 3 weeks parking at LAX was $385.

This is a very irresponsible company; they care less that they can cause the customer a financial or other type of harms.
AVOID THEM; they are not worth your time or your money.< /Text>

Been going to this gym six hours a week for nearly a year now and this is my observations:

Pros:
- Location is good - I enjoy having other gyms to work at when I travel.
- Staff is very nice and friendly
- Never had a trainer, but have met a few and they seem knowledgeable and nice
- Most of the regulars are very friendly and nice

Cons:
- This is the least kept place in all the 24 hour fitness gyms I've been to
- The gym culture does not have very good gym etiquette:  weights are never put back correctly, people will take weights off your rack while you are working out without asking
- People must walk out with the small weights; I spend 5 to 10 minutes a work out session searching for weights that I need
- I have never seen the staff clean up, re-rack weights, or generally keep up after the place
- The mens locker room always seems dirty< /review>

<Name>Sylvia Barela<//Name><Resp>{'time': 1575485083251, 'text': 'Thank you for the 5 star review! Tell your friends!'}< /Resp><Text>Awesome food and very clean...< /Text></record></dataset><record>
<text>Update March 26th 2019: I'm actually going to recommend this place as not only a quick-bite but a decent value for students. My change in tone comes down to one drastic change in policy from previous ownership: to-go boxes.

You can purchase to-go boxes which are reusable and washable. They're a great add on to the value of a meal plan which it seems like they're also changing for the coming fall semester.

Also as I figured the food and ridiculous wait times have since the grand opening settled down, and the food quality has made a leap in quality since the past few years. I'm not sure whether this has to do with new management or a shift from completely relying on student labor to hiring more full-time staff, but they've definitely changed things for the better.

TL;DR It's college food, you can live with it. They serve you the food portioned, but you can good back as many times as you want.  Disappointing remodel.

I've been eating here for 3 years now. In that time, I have worked there for 1, and more recently seen a complete restructure of the service in the most recent academic year (2018-2019).

Let me get this bit out of the way first: it's WAS an on campus cafeteria with primarily students working the kitchen. So yes the food isn't the greatest, but it's edible and can say (believe it or not) a good chunk of the main entrees are prepared fresh. The taste is definitely a hit or miss, but despite a monthly food rotation cycle it gets old fast.

Now I all caps'd "was" because the year I worked there was my first year, and as I mentioned they are no longer run by Spartan Shops. As a result one of the main reasons to actually eat here being the Jamba Juice is gone. In fact a lot of things have been reorganized.

The gluten free kitchen was removed for whatever reason 2 years ago (I know a couple of friends who actually well... CAN'T EAT GLUTEN and were pretty upset when it was removed). Yes they offer gluten free options but for those of us who remembers it's not nearly as satisfying.

The recent remodel currently doesn't have the ice cream machines anymore, there's no more dedicated stand to order coffees, and the cold bar is lacking the variety it had in previous years.

But to their credit, what's left of the relocated desserts bar looks better, there's a wider variety of spices available, and they've added a coffee machine in lieu of the separate stand for ordering it.

Okay I'm stretching quite a bit, and hopefully over time they improve since it seems like they're still in the process of hiring and getting all. the stations setup but until then, it seems this new "Spartan Dining Experience" has turned into more of the same generic food you can find at every other CSU.

I would bring Santa Barbara, Berkeley students, even SJSU alumni and they would be impressed by the DC, because in the past years we really did have it better off than other campuses. Now? I'm not so sure.

Have a meal plan and are dissatisfied with what they  have? Assuming the policy hasn't changed with the new company, in the first few weeks you can always downgrade your plan. I'm considering it, and am hoping it's still an option.

Not that many people would care but I will update this review as and if needed...<//text><username>Carlo del Mundo< /username>< rating>
4< /rating>

<Review>Upon entering this establishment for the first time, I fell under the false assumption of this cafeteria being satisfactory, if not rather extraordinary. However, this facade soon ended, after about a week of decent satisfaction, nothing would've prepared me for what was to come next.

The food available decided to spontaneously contract bipolarism, on some days the food is adequate at best. But, its the other days that I've been warned of. Too many times.

I came in, it was a Tuesday morning, looking for a decent breakfast. I go to get some some eggs, scrambled, as they usually are. Upon first inspection, they seemed fine, but as soon as the yellow fluffy bird-fetus made contact with my taste buds, my eyes squinted, my nose flared, and everything seemed to contract inward. For what I tasted was not egg. No... what I tasted was false hopes and dreams, false promises and legends of true happiness, only to be hit by the bitter truth, like a flame-fisted semi truck hitting my face at high speeds.

So, no. The dining commons is not a good establishment. The opposite actually.

I will leave you with one last story.

Once I wanted to relieve myself, as most would. I entered the mens bathroom, and went to the urinal. But before I could relieve myself, I looked down at the urinal, or atleast what I thought was the urinal. But instead, all I saw was the large disembodied head of Ewan Mcgregor, mouth open awaiting my urine. I proceeded to run away.<//Review><name>Thomas Watkins<//name>< userid>

<user_id>104599907831815339582<//user_id><rating>4</rating><Pics>None</Pics><date>1549852987356</date><user_name>Mark A< /user_name><Response>None<//Response>< Text>
I don‚Äôt often order an omelette. For me, that‚Äôs usually only the safe choice when I can‚Äôt find anything truly appealing. 99% of omelets are scrambled eggs with mediocre ingredients. But for some reason, I was intrigued by the offering at Petite Madeline.

First off, to set the stage, I was ravenous after just completing a long run. Sunday morning post-run breakfast for me is more like an attack by a wild animal than typical human dining. So apologies to the staff if I left a mess ;)

The omelette arrived and immediately it appeared different than what I‚Äôm used to. The egg was delicately folded - more like the dough of a croissant than the typical globular mess of most omelettes. There was a generous portion of the ingredients atop the whole thing and more within. The sausage was absolutely perfect. Full flavored and moist but not the typical acrid assault on the taste buds from cheap breakfast sausage. The goat cheese was perfectly tart and prolifically distributed. Add in spinach and onions, and this was one delightfully flavorful (and filling) meal.

The coffee was also excellent. My girlfriend had a delicious oatmeal bowl that I envied in silence.

Why 4 and not 5 stars? I reserve 5 stars for mind blowing experiences. This was very good and highly recommended. But it‚Äôs not in my top three favorite breakfast places, and I have to draw the line somewhere.</Text>

< text>
This is a cozy little spot in the downtown area of Oceanside. We came here because the place across the street was super busy. For a small little bakery, they were able to accommodate 10 of us in under 10 minutes. Grant it, we were a little tight and really close to our neighboring table, but we were starving so we didn't mind.

The staff here is super friendly and served us very quickly. I ordered a "Mocha de Mexico w/peanuts" which tasted like a hot chocolate with a hint of a peanut flavor. It was decent, but I wish it would have came served a little hotter. The temperature wasn't very hot. I also ordered their two egg breakfast, with wheat toast and homefried potatoes. Their potatoes were delicious! The rest of the breakfast was good too, but the crepes were the hit at the table.

I'm glad we diverted from the place across the street and came here. We were very satisfied with the service and tasty food made from scratch!

(Breakfast served from 7am-3pm)</text>

<user>105646591124249724801< /user><username>Kylie Matsinger<//username><date>1526237989651<//date><rate>1</rate>< Review>
I have come here several times for coffee and a pastry to go. Their coffee is good, they have lots of variety of baked goods and their prices are reasonable. For mother's day, all I wanted to do was finally go here for breakfast and it was such a disappointment. We had to pay for our food and tip before we got any food or service which was different but I tipped 18% assuming their service would be as good as their coffee. Food came relatively fast but they didn't make my husband's pancakes so we had to wait close to 10 minutes for those and my omlette had ham instead of sausage. Not to mention, my entire plate had a THICK layer of oil. My home fries weren't great and I choked through half my omlette that was literally dripping with oil because I had already paid $65 for our food and didn't want to waste it. My husband just got pancakes, hashbrowns and bacon and his was somehow covered in oil too. We are now home and both have stomach aches and regret. Service was dumpy to say the least. I never got a refill on my coffee and had to flag down people for our forgotten food. We were checked on once as we were about to leave but didn't have a set server, it was kinda whoever was around I guess. So sad because I loved this place as a nice coffee stop but I'm never going back.<//Review>
